make[1]: Entering directory '/tmp/libmateweather/src/libmateweather-gtk2/po'
linguas="af am ar as ast az be be@latin bg bn_IN bn br bs ca ca@valencia cmn crh cs cy da de dz el en_AU en_CA en_GB en@shaw eo es_AR es_CL es_CO es_CR es_DO es_EC es_ES es_GT es_HN es_MX es_NI es_PA es_PE es es_PR es_SV es_UY es_VE et eu fa fi fr ga gl gu he hi hr hu hy id is it ja ka kk kn ko ku ky lt lv mai mg mk ml mn mr ms nb nds ne nl nn oc or pa pl pt_BR pt ro ru rw si sk sl sq sr sr@latin sv ta te th tr uk vi wa xh zh_CN zh_HK zh_TW "; \
for lang in $linguas; do \
  dir=/tmp/libmateweather/pkg/libmateweather/usr/share/locale/$lang/LC_MESSAGES; \
  /bin/sh /tmp/libmateweather/src/libmateweather-gtk2/install-sh -d $dir; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo $dir/libmateweather.mo; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo as $dir/libmateweather.mo"; \
  else \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo $dir/libmateweather.mo; \
    echo "installing ./$lang.gmo as" \
	 "$dir/libmateweather.mo"; \
  fi; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo.m; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo.m $dir/libmateweather.mo.m; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo.m as $dir/libmateweather.mo.m"; \
  else \
    if test -r ./$lang.gmo.m ; then \
      /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo.m \
	$dir/libmateweather.mo.m; \
      echo "installing ./$lang.gmo.m as" \
	   "$dir/libmateweather.mo.m"; \
    else \
      true; \
    fi; \

for lang in $linguas; do \
  dir=/tmp/libmateweather/pkg/libmateweather-gtk3/usr/share/locale/$lang/LC_MESSAGES; \
  /bin/sh /tmp/libmateweather/src/libmateweather-gtk3/install-sh -d $dir; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo $dir/libmateweather.mo; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo as $dir/libmateweather.mo"; \
  else \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo $dir/libmateweather.mo; \
    echo "installing ./$lang.gmo as" \
	 "$dir/libmateweather.mo"; \
  fi; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo.m; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo.m $dir/libmateweather.mo.m; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo.m as $dir/libmateweather.mo.m"; \
  else \
    if test -r ./$lang.gmo.m ; then \
      /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo.m \
	$dir/libmateweather.mo.m; \
      echo "installing ./$lang.gmo.m as" \
	   "$dir/libmateweather.mo.m"; \
    else \
      true; \
    fi; \
  fi; \
done
